\newcommand{\proof}{\noindent{\bf Proof.}\ \ }

Number of vertices $n=10$.

Adjacencies of Graph
\begin{enumerate}
\item vertex 1 adjacent to 6 7 8 9 10
\item vertex 2 adjacent to 6 7 8 9 10
\item vertex 3 adjacent to 6 7 8 9 10
\item vertex 4 adjacent to 6 7 8 9 10
\item vertex 5 adjacent to 6 7 8 9 10
\item vertex 6 adjacent to 1 2 3 4 5
\item vertex 7 adjacent to 1 2 3 4 5
\item vertex 8 adjacent to 1 2 3 4 5
\item vertex 9 adjacent to 1 2 3 4 5
\item vertex 10 adjacent to 1 2 3 4 5
\end{enumerate}
Size of automorphism group of the graph=28800

Full group: $\vert Aut(polytope) \vert  =14745600$

Restricted group: $\vert Aut(G) \times switch \vert = 14745600$

Number of orbits for the full group : 1282

List of orbits of facets for the full group:
Total number of orbits = 1282
Total number of facets = 16482678610
\begin{enumerate}

\end{center}
